This includes scholarships, Free Coaching, Economic empowerment schemes and related activities. As the efforts in this direction is significant for upliftment of various sections of the society, there is a need to provide adequate opportunity for candidates to gain expertise and skills in Information Technology, Electronics and related domains which are expected to be leveraged in near future.

ACTIVITY NAME: IIT Bombay FOSSEE GIS Internship in Geospatial Dashboard Design and Implementation

We are happy to announce India's first dedicated internship in Geospatial Dashboard Design and Implementation. This internship is organized/ hosted by the IIT Bombay FOSSEE GIS team, in association with the Rural Data Research and Analysis (RuDRA) Indian Institute of Technology - Bombay (Technical Partner), and IIT Tirupati Navavishkar I-Hub Foundation (Organizing partner).

Last date to apply: August 05, 2023.

Please note:
+ This internship is open 'ONLY' for Indian Nationals.
+ Applicants are required to adhere to the 'National Geospatial Policy (India)',
+ Applicants must be students pursuing studies in any UGC/AICTE-recognized College/ University in India.
+ College pass-outs who have valid degrees from any recognized Indian University or Board can also apply.
+ Students with demonstrated programming (in any Free/Open Source software) skills in dashboard design, with GIS knowledge, shall be given preference.
+ The duration of the internship shall be 06 months (max.). This is subject to the quality of work, and submission of monthly progress reports (before the deadline) and presentations.

+ The 'selected candidates' are required to abide by the standard operating policies of the "IIT Bombay FOSSEE GIS project".
+ The IIT Bombay FOSSEE GIS team shall scrutinize the applications and inform the selected candidates via email.
+ Decisions made by the IIT Bombay FOSSEE GIS team shall be final and non-appealable.

13/08/2023, 09:15 - Amol Jadhav Sir: Dear students, 

To sound better, following are the starting phrases you can use to express your views instead of directly stating your point in a group discussion (GD):

1. "I believe that..."
2. "From my perspective..."
3. "In my opinion..."
4. "I would like to share that..."
5. "As I see it..."
6. "From where I stand..."
7. "In my experience...or In my view I see that..."
8. "It seems to me that..."
9. "Allow me to express..."
10. "In consideration of the topic, I feel that..."
11. "Allow me to offer a perspective that underscores the importance of..."
12. "In contemplating this matter, it becomes evident that..."
13. "As we navigate this topic, it's crucial to recognize..."
14. "Drawing from various sources, it is my contention that..."
15. "Upon careful reflection, one can discern that..."
16. "In light of the complexities involved, I posit that..."
17. "A pertinent point to consider is the impact of..."
18. "Emerging from this discourse is the notion that..."
19. "Considering the broader implications, it's noteworthy that..."
20. "Within the context of our discussion, it's worth noting that..."

09/06/2024, 20:12 - +91 98202 35755: https://risingkashmir.com/aicte-launches-yashasvi-scholarship-to-promote-core-engineering-branches/
Each year, the scholarship will benefit 5,000 students, with 2,500 scholarships allocated for degree students and 2,500 for diploma students. Degree students will receive rupees 18,000 per year for a maximum of four years, while diploma students will receive rupees 12,000 per year for up to three years. Scholarships will be disbursed directly to students via Direct Benefit Transfer (DBT).

Eligibility for the scholarship is based on merit. For degree level students, selection is based on their 12th grade qualifications, while diploma level students are selected based on their 10th grade qualifications. To renew the scholarship each year, students must submit their passing certificate/marksheet along with a letter from the Head of their Institution. Applications for the YASHASVI scholarship will be invited once a year. Eligible candidates are required to apply online on National Scholarship Portal (NSP) after initiation of application process. For more information and application details, please visit the AICTE website.
